[[policy-variant-overloadedbf16-mode-switch-vector-unit-stride-segment-store]]
==== BFloat16 Mode Switch Vector Unit-Stride Segment Store Intrinsics(XAndesVBFHMS)
Intrinsics here don't have a policy variant.

[[policy-variant-overloadedbf16-mode-switch-vector-strided-segment-store]]
==== BFloat16 Mode Switch Vector Strided Segment Store Intrinsics(XAndesVBFHMS)
Intrinsics here don't have a policy variant.

[[policy-variant-overloadedbf16-mode-switch-vector-indexed-segment-load]]
==== BFloat16 Mode Switch Vector Indexed Segment Load Intrinsics(XAndesVBFHMS)

[,c]

[[policy-variant-overloadedbf16-mode-switch-vector-widening-floating-point-fused-multiply-add]]
==== BFloat16 Mode Switch Vector Widening Floating-Point Fused Multiply-Add Intrinsics(XAndesVBFHMS)

[,c]
----
vfloat32mf2_t __riscv_vfwmacc_tu(vfloat32mf2_t vd, vbfloat16mf4_t vs1,
                                 vbfloat16mf4_t vs2, size_t vl);
vfloat32mf2_t __riscv_vfwmacc_tu(vfloat32mf2_t vd, __bf16 vs1,
                                 vbfloat16mf4_t vs2, size_t vl);
vfloat32m1_t __riscv_vfwmacc_tu(vfloat32m1_t vd, vbfloat16mf2_t vs1,
                                vbfloat16mf2_t vs2, size_t vl);
vfloat32m1_t __riscv_vfwmacc_tu(vfloat32m1_t vd, __bf16 vs1, vbfloat16mf2_t vs2,
                                size_t vl);

=== BFloat16 Mode Switch Vector Reduction Operations

[[policy-variant-overloadedbf16-mode-switch-vector-single-width-floating-point-reduction]]
==== BFloat16 Mode Switch Vector Single-Width Floating-Point Reduction Intrinsics(XAndesVBFHMS)

[,c]
----
vbfloat16m1_t __riscv_vfredosum_tu(vbfloat16m1_t vd, vbfloat16mf4_t vs2,
                                   vbfloat16m1_t vs1, size_t vl);
vbfloat16m1_t __riscv_vfredosum_tu(vbfloat16m1_t vd, vbfloat16mf2_t vs2,
                                   vbfloat16m1_t vs1, size_t vl);
vbfloat16m1_t __riscv_vfredosum_tu(vbfloat16m1_t vd, vbfloat16m1_t vs2,
                                   vbfloat16m1_t vs1, size_t vl);
vbfloat16m1_t __riscv_vfredosum_tu(vbfloat16m1_t vd, vbfloat16m2_t vs2,
                                   vbfloat16m1_t vs1, size_t vl);
vbfloat16m1_t __riscv_vfredosum_tu(vbfloat16m1_t vd, vbfloat16m4_t vs2,
                                   vbfloat16m1_t vs1, size_t vl);
vbfloat16m1_t __riscv_vfredosum_tu(vbfloat16m1_t vd, vbfloat16m8_t vs2,
                                   vbfloat16m1_t vs1, size_t vl);

==== BFloat16 Mode Switch Vector Compress Intrinsics(XAndesVBFHMS)

[,c]
----
vbfloat16mf4_t __riscv_vcompress_tu(vbfloat16mf4_t vd, vbfloat16mf4_t vs2,
                                    vbool64_t vs1, size_t vl);
vbfloat16mf2_t __riscv_vcompress_tu(vbfloat16mf2_t vd, vbfloat16mf2_t vs2,
                                    vbool32_t vs1, size_t vl);

                                   vbool16_t vs1, size_t vl);
vbfloat16m2_t __riscv_vcompress_tu(vbfloat16m2_t vd, vbfloat16m2_t vs2,
                                   vbool8_t vs1, size_t vl);

                                   vbool4_t vs1, size_t vl);
vbfloat16m8_t __riscv_vcompress_tu(vbfloat16m8_t vd, vbfloat16m8_t vs2,
                                   vbool2_t vs1, size_t vl);
